```python
def process(data):
    """Process input data."""
    result = []
    for item in data:
        if item.is_valid():
            result.append(item.transform())
    return result
```

#!/bin/bash

```python
def process(data):
    """Process input data."""
    result = []
    for item in data:
        if item.is_valid():
            result.append(item.transform())
    return result
```

#!/bin/bash
set -euo pipefail

```python
def process(data):
    """Process input data."""
    result = []
    for item in data:
        if item.is_valid():
            result.append(item.transform())
    return result
```

```python
def process(data):
    """Process input data."""
    result = []
    for item in data:
        if item.is_valid():
            result.append(item.transform())
    return result
```

```python
def process(data):
    """Process input data."""
    result = []
    for item in data:
        if item.is_valid():
            result.append(item.transform())
    return result
```

```python
def process(data):
    """Process input data."""
    result = []
    for item in data:
        if item.is_valid():
            result.append(item.transform())
    return result
```

```python
def process(data):
    """Process input data."""
    result = []
    for item in data:
        if item.is_valid():
            result.append(item.transform())
    return result
```

```python
def process(data):
    """Process input data."""
    result = []
    for item in data:
        if item.is_valid():
            result.append(item.transform())
    return result
```

function fetchData(url) {
  return fetch(url)
    .then(res => res.json())
    .then(data => data.results);

```python
def process(data):
    """Process input data."""
    result = []
    for item in data:
        if item.is_valid():
            result.append(item.transform())
    return result
```

```python
def process(data):
    """Process input data."""
    result = []
    for item in data:
        if item.is_valid():
            result.append(item.transform())
    return result
```

```python
def process(data):
    """Process input data."""
    result = []
    for item in data:
        if item.is_valid():
            result.append(item.transform())
    return result
```

```python
def process(data):
    """Process input data."""
    result = []
    for item in data:
        if item.is_valid():
            result.append(item.transform())
    return result
```

```python
def process(data):
    """Process input data."""
    result = []
    for item in data:
        if item.is_valid():
            result.append(item.transform())
    return result
```
